    <script src="js/5.2.2-lazysizes.min.js"></script>

  
    <script>
        $(".loc-toggle").click(function () {
            $(window).width() <= 991 && $(".b_e519").fadeToggle(300)
        });
    </script>
    <script>
        $(".loc-pc-toggle").click(function () {
            $(window).width() >= 767 && $(".loc-dropdn").fadeToggle(300)
        });
    </script>
    <script>
        $('.single-item').slick({
            slidesToShow: 1,
            slidesToScroll: 1,
            autoplay: true,
            fade: true,
            autoplaySpeed: 1900,
        });
    </script>
    <script>
        $('.autoplay').slick({
            lazyLoad: 'progressive',
            slidesToShow: 4,
            slidesToScroll: 1,
            arrow: true,
            prevArrow: '<button class="slick-next slick-arrow icon-arrow-right" type="button">',
            nextArrow: '<button class="slick-prev slick-arrow icon-arrow-left" type="button">',
            responsive: [{
                breakpoint: 1024,
                settings: {
                    centerMode: true,
                    centerPadding: '10px',
                    slidesToShow: 4
                }
            },
            {
                breakpoint: 768,
                settings: {
                    centerMode: true,
                    centerPadding: '10px',
                    slidesToShow: 3
                }
            },
            {
                breakpoint: 480,
                settings: {
                    centerMode: true,
                    centerPadding: '10px',
                    slidesToShow: 2
                }
            }
            ]
        });
    </script> 
    <script>
        $(document).ready(function () {


            $('.scroll-top').click(function () {
                $("html, body").animate({
                    scrollTop: 0
                }, 1000);
                return false;
            });



        });
    </script>
